 Lucknow, August 11: Language: In Uttar Pradesh, no person will now have any claim for the return of land acquired by the state government
 bhale hi vah bhoomi kitne bhi samay tak khaali padi rahe
 The law so far applicable in the state provides that if the state government does not use any land within five years from the date of its acquisition and the land remains vacant then its former owner will get the land with certain conditions from the state government
 Could demand to get back
 pradesh sarkaar ne maujuuda adhinium ke us praavdhaan ko sanshodhit karne ke liye rajya vidhansabha main ‘‘uttar pradesh nagar yojana or vikaas :sanshodhan: vidheyak 2011’’ prastut kiya tha or aaj sadan main yah sanshodhan vidheyak dhvanimat se paarit kar diya gaya he
 Section 17 of the present Act provides for compulsory land acquisition and its sub-section (1) also provides that if the acquired land is not used for declared purpose within five years and the land remains vacant then its former owner
 He could claim to get his land back by returning the money received as a reimbursement amount to the government with 12 percent interest
 sadan main aaj paarit sanshodhan karke yah vyavastha kar di gayi he ki arjeet kii gayi bhoomi ke bhu-swami bhavishya main apni jameen kii vaapasi ke liye koi daawa nahin kar sakenge

 darasal, kendriya vitt mantri nirmala sitaraman ne bajet pesh karte hue kaha ki sarkaar saarvajanik kshetra ke companiyon kii ''ranneetik vinievesh'' karegi

 Understand in easy language, the government withdraws money from one account and buys shares of its own company from another account
 kya hoti he vinievesh prakriyavinivesh prakriya nivesh kaa ulataa hota he
 Where investment is to be invested in a business, an institution or a project, then disinvestment means withdrawing that amount
 yahaan nijeekaran or vinievesh ke antar ko samajhnaa jaruri he
 In privatization, the government sells more than 51 per cent of its stake to the private sector, while in the process of disinvestment, it acquires some of its share, but its ownership remains, but will no longer survive in "strategic disinvestment"
